11.　God's economy is God's plan and arrangement out of His desire and purpose, God's economy in relation to His good pleasure, will, counsel, and purpose—2:4; Rev. 4:11.
12.　God's eternal economy is to make man the same as He is in life and nature but not in the Godhead and to make Himself one with man and man one with Him, thus, to be enlarged and expanded in His expression, that all His divine attributes may be expressed in human virtues—Eph. 4:18; John 3:16; Col. 1:19.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十三篇　神经纶的中心点
The Focus of God's Economy
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：弗一10，三9，西一15、19、27，罗一3~4，八3，提前一4下
壹　神圣的经纶是神成为人，为要使人在生命和性情上，但不在神格上，成为神，以产生三一神的生机体，基督的身体，这身体要终极完成于新耶路撒冷─罗一3~4，八3、6、10~11、16，十二4~5，启二一2、10~11：
I.　The divine economy is that God became man so that man may become God in life and nature but not in the Godhead to produce the organism of the Triune God, the Body of Christ, which consummates in the New Jerusalem— Rom. 1:3-4; 8:3, 6, 10-11, 16; 12:4-5; Rev. 21:2, 10-11:
一　神圣的经纶乃是出于神的意愿、定旨、喜悦和决议─弗一5、9~11，三9~11：
A.　The divine economy is the issue of God's will, purpose, good pleasure, and counsel— Eph. 1:5, 9-11; 3:9-11:
1　神的意愿乃是神的愿望，神的渴望；神的意愿是祂所愿望要作的，和祂所想要作的─启四11，弗一5。
1.　God's will is God's wish, God's desire; God's will is what He wishes to do and wants to do—Rev. 4:11; Eph. 1:5.
2　神的定旨乃是神预先所定的目的；神永远的定旨是祂在已过的永远里所定的永远计划─9节，三11。
2.　God's purpose is God's intent set beforehand; God's eternal purpose is His eternal plan made in eternity past—v. 9; 3:11.
3　神的喜悦乃是使神喜乐的；那是神所喜爱、讨祂欢喜的─一5、9，腓二13。
3.　God's good pleasure is what makes God happy; it is what God likes and what pleases Him—1:5, 9; Phil. 2:13.
4　神的决议乃是神在神圣三一的会议中所完成的定议─弗一9，徒二23，彼前一20。
4.　God's counsel is God's resolution consummated in the council of the Divine Trinity—Eph. 1:9; Acts 2:23; 1 Pet. 1:20.
5　在神的意愿、定旨、喜悦、和决议之后，就是神的经纶─神的家庭行政，神的计划与安排─提前一4，弗一10，三9。
5.　After God's will, purpose, good pleasure, and counsel, there is God's economy— God's household administration, God's plan and arrangement—1 Tim. 1:4; Eph. 1:10; 3:9.
二　神圣的经纶就是神成为肉体，经过人生，受死，复活，成为赐生命的灵，进到我们里面作生命，把神分赐到我们里面，叫我们得变化，以产生召会，就是基督的身体─约一14、29，徒二24，林前十二12~13，十五45下，提前三15，启五10，二一2。
B.　The divine economy is that God became flesh, passed through human living, died, resurrected, and became the life-giving Spirit to enter into us as life and to dispense God into us so that we may be transformed for the producing of the church, which is the Body of Christ—John 1:14, 29; Acts 2:24; 1 Cor. 12:12-13; 15:45b; 1 Tim. 3:15; Rev. 5:10; 21:2.
贰　神圣经纶的完成乃是借着神圣三一的神圣分赐─林后十三14，弗一3~23，三14~21：
II.　The accomplishment of the divine economy is by the divine dispensing of the Divine Trinity—2 Cor. 13:14; Eph. 1:3-23; 3:14-21:
一　神圣的经纶乃是神的计划和安排，出自神的渴望和定旨；神圣的分赐乃是按照这计划和安排而有的神的分赐并授与─一5、9~11，三14~17上。
A.　The divine economy is God's plan and arrangement of His desire and purpose; the divine dispensing is God's dispensing and distributing according to this plan and arrangement—1:5, 9-11; 3:14-17a.
二　新约里说到关于神的一切事，都与那为着神圣经纶的神圣分赐有关─罗八3、11，弗一3~23：
B.　Everything that is mentioned in the New Testament concerning God is related to the divine dispensing for the divine economy—Rom. 8:3, 11; Eph. 1:3-23:
1　圣言中关于三一神的启示，不是为着道理的明白，而是为着神在祂的神圣三一里，分赐到祂所拣选、救赎的人里面，给他们经历并享受─林后十三14。
1.　The revelation concerning the Triune God in the holy Word is not for doctrinal understanding but for the dispensing of God in His Divine Trinity into His chosen and redeemed people for their experience and enjoyment—2 Cor. 13:14.
2　三一神─父、子、灵─经过了过程，成为赐生命的灵，使我们能饮于祂，使祂能成为我们的享受；这就是神圣三一的神圣分赐─约七37~39。
2.　The Triune God—the Father, the Son, and the Spirit—has been processed to become the life-giving Spirit so that we can drink of Him and that He can be-come our enjoyment; this is the divine dispensing of the Divine Trinity—John 7:37-39.
3　神圣的三一乃是为着神圣的分赐，就是将神分授到在基督里的信徒里面；父是起源，就是源；子是彰显，就是泉；灵是传输，就是流─四14。
3.　The Divine Trinity is for the divine dispensing, that is, for the distribution of God into the believers in Christ; the Father as the origin is the fountain, the Son as the expression is the spring, and the Spirit as the transmission is the flow—4:14.
叁　包罗万有的基督是神经纶的中心点─西一27，提前三15~16：
III.　The all-inclusive Christ is the focus of God's economy—Col. 1:27; 1 Tim. 3:15-16:
一　神的经纶是在信仰里的，就是在信仰的范围和元素里得以开始而发展的─一4下。
A.　The economy of God is a matter in faith, that is initiated and developed in the sphere and element of the faith—1:4b.
二　神的经纶有诸多方面：
B.　God's economy has many aspects:
1　经纶是一种作事的安排。
1.　An economy is an arrangement for getting things done.
2　神的经纶是神的家庭管理，神的家庭行政安排─弗一10，三9。
2.　God's economy is God's household management, God's household administrative arrangement—Eph. 1:10; 3:9.
3　神的经纶是祂所计划的行政，为要完成祂永远的定旨─约十四23。
3.　God's economy is God's planned administration to carry out His eternal purpose—John 14:23.
4　神的经纶是神在信仰里在基督里分授祂自己─西一15，提前一4下。
4.　God's economy is God's distribution of Himself in Christ in faith—Col. 1:15; 1 Tim. 1:4b.
5　神的经纶是神的计划，要将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选、预定、并救赎的人里面，作他们的生命、生命的供应和一切─弗四6，罗八11。
5.　God's economy is God's plan to dispense Himself into His chosen, predestinated, and redeemed people as their life, their life supply, and their everything—Eph. 4:6; Rom. 8:11.
6　神的经纶是神的家庭行政，要将三一神的神圣丰富，作为生命和生命的供应，分赐到祂所拣选并救赎的人里面─林后十三14。
6.　God's economy is God's household administration to dispense the divine riches of the Triune God as life and the life supply to His chosen and redeemed people—2 Cor. 13:14.
7　神的经纶不是外面的事，乃是使基督进入我们里面作食物─约六31~35、63，七37，林前五8。
7.　God's economy is not a matter of outward things but of Christ coming into us as food—John 6:31-35, 63; 7:37; 1 Cor. 5:8.
8　神的经纶是要我们吃基督，并由祂所构成─约六57，林前十3~4，彼前二2。
8.　God's economy is that we eat Christ and become constituted with Christ— John 6:57; 1 Cor. 10:3-4; 1 Pet. 2:2.
9　神的经纶是三一神要把祂自己，作到我们这三部分的人里面；祂要作我们的生命、内容和一切的供应，使我们成为神的彰显和代表─约壹三2，腓三21。
9.　The economy of God is the Triune God working Himself into us, the tripartite men; He desires to be our life, content, and complete supply so that we would become God's expression and representation—1 John 3:2; Phil. 3:21.
10　神的经纶就是祂这位三一神要把祂自己作到我们里面，使我们有祂的生命和性情，成为神的众子，和基督的众肢体，构成基督的身体，就是召会，基督的彰显─西一27，提前三15~16。
10.　God's economy is to work Himself as the Triune God into us so that we would have His life and nature to become the sons of God and the members of Christ to be constituted the Body of Christ, which is the church, the expression of Christ—Col. 1:27; 1 Tim. 3:15-16.
11　神的经纶是出于神心愿和定旨的计划并安排，就是神与祂的喜悦、旨意、决议和定旨有关的经纶─二4，启四11。
11.　God's economy is God's plan and arrangement out of His desire and purpose, God's economy in relation to His good pleasure, will, counsel, and purpose—2:4; Rev. 4:11.
12　神永远的经纶，是要使人在生命和性情上，但不在神格上，与祂一样，并要使祂与人成为一，也使人与祂成为一，因而使祂在彰显上得以扩大并扩展，使祂一切神圣的属性得以彰显在人性美德里─弗四18，约三16，西一19。
12.　God's eternal economy is to make man the same as He is in life and nature but not in the Godhead and to make Himself one with man and man one with Him, thus, to be enlarged and expanded in His expression, that all His divine attributes may be expressed in human virtues—Eph. 4:18; John 3:16; Col. 1:19.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第十四篇　为着一个新人，让基督的平安在我们心里作仲裁，让基督的话丰丰富富的住在我们里面，以及坚定持续的祷告
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：西三15～17，四2～4
壹　“要让基督的平安在你们心里作仲裁，你们在一个身体里蒙召，也是为了这平安；且要感恩”─西三12～15，二14～18：
一　基督的平安要在我们心里作仲裁，倘若这人与那人有嫌隙，就需要“彼此容忍，彼此饶恕；主怎样饶恕了你们，你们也要怎样饶恕人”─三13：
1　饶恕人的主是我们的生命，且活在我们里面；饶恕是祂生命的一种美德；当我们以祂作我们的生命和人位，并凭祂活着，饶恕人就是自然的，就成了我们基督徒生活的一种美德。
2　我们也该向主感恩；在基督身体的生活中，我们的心向着众肢体总该是在平安的情形里，并且向着主也总该感恩。
二　“作仲裁”，原文或，“作裁判，作主席，登位作每件事的管治者和决断者；”基督那在我们心里作仲裁的平安，消除了我们对任何人的嫌隙─15、13节。
三　我们常常发现我们里面有三派：一派是积极的，另一派是消极的，还有一派是中立的；因此，需要内里的仲裁来解决我们里面的争执：
1　每当我们感觉我们里面各派在争执时，就需要让基督的平安作主席，并让这平安，就是新人的一，在我们里面管治并下最后的断语。
2　我们需要把我们的意见、观念摆在一边，听内住之裁判的话。
四　我们若让基督的平安在我们心里作仲裁，这平安会解决我们中间所有的争执，我们就会与神有纵的平安，并与圣徒有横的平安：
1　借着基督的平安作仲裁，我们的难处解决了，圣徒之间的摩擦也消失了；然后召会生活就能甜美的得保全，新人也实际的得以维持。
2　基督的平安作仲裁，就是基督在我们里面作工，好在我们身上施行管治，来作结论，下最后的决断─参赛九6～7。
3　如果我们一直让基督的平安作王管治，我们就不会得罪别人，破坏别人；我们反而会靠着主的恩典连同祂的平安，把生命供应给别人─约壹五16上。
4　这平安应当将所有的信徒联结一起，成为和平的联索─弗四3。
五　我们不但该让基督的平安在心里作仲裁，也该向主感恩；在基督身体的生活中，我们的心向着众肢体总该是在平安的情形里，并且也该为着主每天的看顾和拯救向主感恩─西三15下，诗一○七1～2、8、15、21、31～32。
贰　“让基督的话丰丰富富的住在你们里面”─西三16～17：
一　在歌罗西书，基督的话是为着启示基督（一25～27）的居首、中心和普及（16～17）。─引用经文
二　基督的话丰丰富富的住在我们里面，意思是基督的话在我们里面有充分的地位，好浸润并浸透我们全人；我们必须让基督的话进到我们里面，住在我们里面，在我们里面胜过一切，并顶替我们的观念、意见和哲学，这是极其重要的─诗一一九130，参启二一23，二二5。
三　我们需要让主的话在我们里面居首位，使我们经历神话语的功用在我们里面运行─西三16：
1　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是将活神供应给寻求祂的人─诗一一九2、88。
2　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是将神自己作为生命和光，分赐到那些爱神的话之人里面─25、50、107、116、130、154节。
3　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是苏醒人的魂，快活人的心─十九7～8。
4　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是带来救恩─一一九41、170。
5　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是使我们坚立（28），安慰我们（76），并滋养我们（103）。─引用经文
6　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是扶持我们，使我们得救，并使我们有盼望─116～117、49节。
7　神活的话，基督的话，使我们享受神作我们的业分─57节。
8　神活的话，基督的话，使我们享受神的面（58），以及祂脸上的光照（135）。─引用经文
9　神活的话，基督的话，使我们享受神作我们的藏身之处和盾牌（114），也享受神的帮助和善待（175、65）。─引用经文
10　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是使我们有智慧并且通达─98～99节。
11　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是赐给我们正确的明辨和知识─66节。
12　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是保守我们不犯罪，不走一切的邪路─11、101节。
13　神活的话，基督的话，保守我们不绊跌（165），使我们的脚步稳当，并使我们胜过罪孽─133节。
14　神活的话，基督的话，纯净我们并将我们美化为祂的新妇─十二6，一一九140，弗五26～27，赛六十7下，21，诗二七4。
四　神的话在我们的经历中对我们是不是光，乃在于我们来到神话语前的态度和光景─约五39～40：
1　我们需要谦卑自己，不信靠自己，只仰望主的怜悯─赛五七15，六六2。
2　我们全人的各部分应当敞开，接受主的光照─箴二十27。
五　我们不该制造光，乃该倚靠主光照我们─赛五十10～11。
叁　“你们要坚定持续的祷告”─西四2～4：
一　我们若照着主在路加十一章一至十三节的教导祷告，结果我们就会把自己祷告到神里面：─引用经文
1　在我们的经历中，我们常受打岔离开神；我们没有住在神里面─我们没有停留在神里面；这就是为什么我们需要把自己祷告到神里面。
2　因为我们很容易受打岔离开神，所以我们应当每天早晨花时间与祂同在，把自己祷告到祂里面─诗五3，赛五十4。
3　我们祷告的方式若打岔我们，使我们离开主，没有把我们带到主里面，我们祷告的方式就当改变，好把自己祷告到祂里面。
4　当我们把自己祷告到神里面，我们就领受祂的丰富（由饼、鱼和鸡蛋所代表）到我们里面，作我们的供应─路十一5～13。
5　饼代表地上的丰富；鱼代表海里的丰富；鸡蛋代表空中与地上之物的丰富；圣灵是这些丰富的总和。
6　当我们把自己祷告到神里面，而停留在神里面，我们就接受圣灵作我们生命的供应（由饼、鱼和鸡蛋所表征），使我们能喂养自己，也能喂养一切受我们照顾的人─太二四45～46，约壹五16上，林后三6，徒六4。
7　我们需要有充分的时间祷告，以确定并有效能的方式私下、隐密的接触主─路十一13，太十四22～23，六6。
二　祷告的意思是说，我们看见自己一无所是，一无所能；这含示祷告是真正的否认己─可八34，九29，西四2，加二20，腓三3，四6～7、11～13。
三　祷告实际上就是宣告：“不再是我，乃是基督；”我们的祷告见证我们没有靠自己的努力，去应付任何处境─加二20，罗十12～13。
四　即使在最小的事上，我们都需要求问主；这样作，就是坚定持续的祷告，并因此而活基督─诗二七4，参书九14，腓四7～8。
五　我们需要划出定时祷告的时间；我们的态度应当把祷告当作我们最重要的事，不让任何的事情打岔─但六10，徒十二5、12。
六　我们要神垂听我们的祷告，就必须向着圣地、圣城、和圣殿所表征之神的权益祷告─王上八48：
1　圣地，预表基督是神分给信徒的分（西一12，二6～7，申八7）；圣城，表征在基督里神的国（诗四八1～2）；圣殿，表征神在地上的家，召会（弗二21，提前三15）。─引用经文
2　在被掳到巴比伦期间，但以理把窗户开向耶路撒冷，一日三次祷告；这指明当我们向神的祷告是向着神永远经纶里的目标，就是基督、神的国、与神的家时，神必垂听我们的祷告─但六10。
3　这意思是说，不论我们为谁祷告，我们的祷告都该对准神的权益，就是对准基督与召会─神在地上的权益，以完成神的经纶。
肆　我们借着坚定持续的祷告而受基督的平安管治，并被基督的话内住，祂就以祂自己浸润我们，并顶替我们，直到我们一切天然的区别都被消除，我们就在实际里成为新人─西三15～17，四2～3，三10～11。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
THE CRUCIAL POINTS OF THE TRUTH IN PAUL'S EPISTLES— PHILIPPIANS AND COLOSSIANS
Message Fourteen
Allowing the Peace of Christ to Arbitrate in Our Hearts, Letting the Word of Christ Dwell in Us Richly, and Persevering in Prayer for the One New Man
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: Col. 3:15-17; 4:2-4
I.　"Let the peace of Christ arbitrate in your hearts, to which also you were called in one Body; and be thankful"—Col. 3:12-15; 2:14-18:
A.　In order for the peace of Christ to arbitrate in our hearts, we need to be those who are "bearing one another and forgiving one another, if anyone should have a complaint against anyone; even as the Lord forgave you, so also should you forgive"—3:13:
1.　The forgiving Lord is our life and lives within us; forgiving is a virtue of His life; when we take Him as our life and person and live by Him, our forgiving of others will be spontaneous—it will become a virtue of our Christian life.
2.　We should also be thankful to the Lord; in the Body life our heart should always be in a peaceful condition toward the members and should be thankful to the Lord.
B.　The Greek term for arbitrate can also be rendered "umpire, preside, be enthroned as a ruler and decider of everything"; the arbitrating peace of Christ in our hearts dissolves our complaint against anyone—vv. 15, 13.
C.　Often we are conscious of three parties within us: a positive party, a negative party, and a neutral party; hence, there is the need for inward arbitration to settle the dispute within us:
1.　Whenever we sense that different parties within our being are arguing, we need to give place to the presiding peace of Christ and allow this peace, which is the oneness of the new man, to rule within us and have the final word.
2.　We need to set aside our opinion, our concept, and listen to the word of the indwelling referee.
D.　If we allow the peace of Christ to arbitrate in our hearts, this peace will settle all the disputes among us; we will have peace with God vertically and with the saints horizontally:
1.　Through the arbitration of the peace of Christ, our problems are solved, and the friction between the saints disappears; then the church life is preserved in sweetness, and the new man is maintained in a practical way.
2.　The arbitrating of the peace of Christ is Christ working within us to exercise His rule over us, to speak the last word, and to make the final decision—cf. Isa. 9:6-7.
3.　If we stay under the ruling of the enthroned peace of Christ, we will not offend others or damage them; rather, by the Lord's grace and with His peace, we will minister life to others—1 John 5:16a.
4.　This peace should bind all the believers together and become the uniting bond of peace—Eph. 4:3.
E.　We not only should let the peace of Christ arbitrate in our hearts, but we also should be thankful to the Lord; in the Body life our heart should always be in a peaceful condition toward the members and should be thankful to the Lord for His care and saving every day—Col. 3:15b; Psa. 107:1-2, 8, 15, 21, 31-32.
II.　"Let the word of Christ dwell in you richly"—Col. 3:16-17:
A.　The word of Christ in Colossians is for revealing Christ (1:25-27) in His preeminence, centrality, and universality (vv. 16-17).
B.　For the word of Christ to dwell in us richly means that it has adequate room in us to permeate and saturate our whole being; it is crucial for us to let the word of Christ enter into us, dwell in us, prevail in us, and replace our concepts, opinions, and philosophies— Psa. 119:130; cf. Rev. 21:23; 22:5.
C.　We need to allow the word of the Lord to have the first place in us so that we may experience the functions of the word of God operating within us—Col. 3:16:
1.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to minister the living God to His seekers—Psa. 119:2, 88.
2.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to dispense God Himself as life and light into those who love the word—vv. 25, 50, 107, 116, 130, 154.
3.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to restore man's soul and make man's heart joyous—19:7-8.
4.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to bring us salvation—119:41, 170.
5.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to strengthen (v. 28), comfort (v. 76), and nourish us (v. 103).
6.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to uphold us, keep us safe, and cause us to hope—vv. 116-117, 49.
7.　God's living word, the word of Christ, causes us to enjoy God as our portion—v. 57.
8.　God's living word, the word of Christ, causes us to enjoy God's countenance (v. 58) and the shining of His face (v. 135).
9.　God's living word, the word of Christ, causes us to enjoy God as our hiding place and shield (v. 114) and also enjoy God's help and well-dealing (vv. 175, 65).
10.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to make us wise and give us under-standing—vv. 98-99.
11.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to give us proper discernment and knowledge—v. 66.
12.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to keep us from sinning and from every evil way—vv. 11, 101.
13.　God's living word, the word of Christ, keeps us from stumbling (v. 165), establishes our footsteps, and causes us to overcome iniquity (v. 133).
14.　God's living word, the word of Christ, purifies us and beautifies us to be His bride— 12:6; 119:140; Eph. 5:26-27; Isa. 60:7b, 21; Psa. 27:4.
D.　Whether or not God's word is a light to us in our experience depends on our attitude and condition in coming to the Word—John 5:39-40:
1.　We need to humble ourselves, having no confidence in ourselves but looking to the Lord for mercy—Isa. 57:15; 66:2.
2.　All the chambers of our inner being should be open to receive the Lord's shining— Prov. 20:27.
E.　We should not manufacture light; instead, we should rely on the Lord to enlighten us— Isa. 50:10-11.
III.　"Persevere in prayer"—Col. 4:2-4:
A.　If we pray according to the Lord's instructions in Luke 11:1-13, the result will be that we pray ourselves into God:
1.　Often in our experience we are distracted from God; we do not stay in God—we do not remain in Him; this is why we need to pray ourselves into God.
2.　Because we are easily distracted from God, we should spend time every morning with Him, praying ourselves into Him—Psa. 5:3; Isa. 50:4.
3.　If our way of praying distracts us from the Lord and does not bring us into Him, we should change our way of praying so that we pray ourselves into Him.
4.　When we pray ourselves into God, we receive His riches (represented by the loaves, the fish, and the egg) into our being for our supply—Luke 11:5-13.
5.　Loaves represent the riches of the land; fish, the riches of the sea; and eggs, the riches of something both in the air and on the earth; the Holy Spirit is the totality of these riches.
6.　When we have prayed ourselves into God to remain in Him, we receive the Holy Spirit as our life supply (signified by the loaves, the fish, and the egg) so that we can feed ourselves and all those under our care—Matt. 24:45-46; 1 John 5:16a; 2 Cor. 3:6; Acts 6:4.
7.　We need to allow adequate time for prayer, contacting Him privately and secretly in a definite and prevailing way—Luke 11:13; Matt. 14:22-23; 6:6.
B.　To pray means that we realize that we are nothing and that we can do nothing; this implies that prayer is the real denial of the self—Mark 8:34; 9:29; Col. 4:2; Gal. 2:20; Phil. 3:3; 4:6-7, 11-13.
C.　To pray is actually to declare, "No longer I, but Christ"; our prayer testifies that we do not exercise our self-effort to deal with any situation—Gal. 2:20; Rom. 10:12-13.
D.　Even in the smallest details we need to inquire of the Lord; to do this is to persevere in prayer and thereby to live Christ—Psa. 27:4; cf. Josh. 9:14; Phil. 4:7-8.
E.　We need to set aside definite times for prayer; our attitude should be that prayer is our most important business and that nothing should be allowed to interfere with it—Dan. 6:10; Acts 12:5, 12.
F.　In order for God to listen to our prayers, we need to pray toward God's interests, signified by the Holy Land, the holy city, and the holy temple—1 Kings 8:48:
1.　The Holy Land typifies Christ as the portion allotted by God to the believers (Col. 1:12; 2:6-7; Deut. 8:7); the holy city signifies the kingdom of God in Christ (Psa. 48:1-2); and the holy temple signifies God's house, the church, on the earth (Eph. 2:21; 1 Tim. 3:15).
2.　During the Babylonian captivity Daniel prayed three times a day by opening his windows toward Jerusalem; this indicates that God will listen to our prayer when our prayer to God is toward Christ, the kingdom of God, and the house of God as the goal in God's eternal economy—Dan. 6:10.
3.　This means that no matter for whom we are praying, our prayers should be aimed at the interests of God, that is, at Christ and the church as God's interests on earth, for the fulfilling of God's economy.
IV.　As we are ruled by the peace of Christ and inhabited by the word of Christ through persevering in prayer, He permeates and replaces us with Himself until all our natural distinctions have been eliminated and we become the new man in reality— Col. 3:15-17; 4:2-3; 3:10-11.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十四篇　为着一个新人，让基督的平安在我们心里作仲裁，让基督的话丰丰富富的住在我们里面，以及坚定持续的祷告
Allowing the Peace of Christ to Arbitrate in Our Hearts, Letting the Word of Christ Dwell in Us Richly, and Persevering in Prayer for the One New Man
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：西三15～17，四2～4
壹　“要让基督的平安在你们心里作仲裁，你们在一个身体里蒙召，也是为了这平安；且要感恩”─西三12～15，二14～18：
I.　"Let the peace of Christ arbitrate in your hearts, to which also you were called in one Body; and be thankful"—Col. 3:12-15; 2:14-18:
一　基督的平安要在我们心里作仲裁，倘若这人与那人有嫌隙，就需要“彼此容忍，彼此饶恕；主怎样饶恕了你们，你们也要怎样饶恕人”─三13：
A.　In order for the peace of Christ to arbitrate in our hearts, we need to be those who are "bearing one another and forgiving one another, if anyone should have a complaint against anyone; even as the Lord forgave you, so also should you forgive"—3:13:
1　饶恕人的主是我们的生命，且活在我们里面；饶恕是祂生命的一种美德；当我们以祂作我们的生命和人位，并凭祂活着，饶恕人就是自然的，就成了我们基督徒生活的一种美德。
1.　The forgiving Lord is our life and lives within us; forgiving is a virtue of His life; when we take Him as our life and person and live by Him, our forgiving of others will be spontaneous—it will become a virtue of our Christian life.
2　我们也该向主感恩；在基督身体的生活中，我们的心向着众肢体总该是在平安的情形里，并且向着主也总该感恩。
2.　We should also be thankful to the Lord; in the Body life our heart should always be in a peaceful condition toward the members and should be thankful to the Lord.
二　“作仲裁”，原文或，“作裁判，作主席，登位作每件事的管治者和决断者；”基督那在我们心里作仲裁的平安，消除了我们对任何人的嫌隙─15、13节。
B.　The Greek term for arbitrate can also be rendered "umpire, preside, be enthroned as a ruler and decider of everything"; the arbitrating peace of Christ in our hearts dissolves our complaint against anyone—vv. 15, 13.
三　我们常常发现我们里面有三派：一派是积极的，另一派是消极的，还有一派是中立的；因此，需要内里的仲裁来解决我们里面的争执：
C.　Often we are conscious of three parties within us: a positive party, a negative party, and a neutral party; hence, there is the need for inward arbitration to settle the dispute within us:
1　每当我们感觉我们里面各派在争执时，就需要让基督的平安作主席，并让这平安，就是新人的一，在我们里面管治并下最后的断语。
1.　Whenever we sense that different parties within our being are arguing, we need to give place to the presiding peace of Christ and allow this peace, which is the oneness of the new man, to rule within us and have the final word.
2　我们需要把我们的意见、观念摆在一边，听内住之裁判的话。
2.　We need to set aside our opinion, our concept, and listen to the word of the indwelling referee.
四　我们若让基督的平安在我们心里作仲裁，这平安会解决我们中间所有的争执，我们就会与神有纵的平安，并与圣徒有横的平安：
D.　If we allow the peace of Christ to arbitrate in our hearts, this peace will settle all the disputes among us; we will have peace with God vertically and with the saints horizontally:
1　借着基督的平安作仲裁，我们的难处解决了，圣徒之间的摩擦也消失了；然后召会生活就能甜美的得保全，新人也实际的得以维持。
1.　Through the arbitration of the peace of Christ, our problems are solved, and the friction between the saints disappears; then the church life is preserved in sweetness, and the new man is maintained in a practical way.
2　基督的平安作仲裁，就是基督在我们里面作工，好在我们身上施行管治，来作结论，下最后的决断─参赛九6～7。
2.　The arbitrating of the peace of Christ is Christ working within us to exercise His rule over us, to speak the last word, and to make the final decision—cf. Isa. 9:6-7.
3　如果我们一直让基督的平安作王管治，我们就不会得罪别人，破坏别人；我们反而会靠着主的恩典连同祂的平安，把生命供应给别人─约壹五16上。
3.　If we stay under the ruling of the enthroned peace of Christ, we will not offend others or damage them; rather, by the Lord's grace and with His peace, we will minister life to others—1 John 5:16a.
4　这平安应当将所有的信徒联结一起，成为和平的联索─弗四3。
4.　This peace should bind all the believers together and become the uniting bond of peace—Eph. 4:3.
五　我们不但该让基督的平安在心里作仲裁，也该向主感恩；在基督身体的生活中，我们的心向着众肢体总该是在平安的情形里，并且也该为着主每天的看顾和拯救向主感恩─西三15下，诗一○七1～2、8、15、21、31～32。
E.　We not only should let the peace of Christ arbitrate in our hearts, but we also should be thankful to the Lord; in the Body life our heart should always be in a peaceful condition toward the members and should be thankful to the Lord for His care and saving every day—Col. 3:15b; Psa. 107:1-2, 8, 15, 21, 31-32.
贰　“让基督的话丰丰富富的住在你们里面”─西三16～17：
II.　"Let the word of Christ dwell in you richly"—Col. 3:16-17:
一　在歌罗西书，基督的话是为着启示基督（一25～27）的居首、中心和普及（16～17）。─引用经文
A.　The word of Christ in Colossians is for revealing Christ (1:25-27) in His preeminence, centrality, and universality (vv. 16-17).
二　基督的话丰丰富富的住在我们里面，意思是基督的话在我们里面有充分的地位，好浸润并浸透我们全人；我们必须让基督的话进到我们里面，住在我们里面，在我们里面胜过一切，并顶替我们的观念、意见和哲学，这是极其重要的─诗一一九130，参启二一23，二二5。
B.　For the word of Christ to dwell in us richly means that it has adequate room in us to permeate and saturate our whole being; it is crucial for us to let the word of Christ enter into us, dwell in us, prevail in us, and replace our concepts, opinions, and philosophies— Psa. 119:130; cf. Rev. 21:23; 22:5.
三　我们需要让主的话在我们里面居首位，使我们经历神话语的功用在我们里面运行─西三16：
C.　We need to allow the word of the Lord to have the first place in us so that we may experience the functions of the word of God operating within us—Col. 3:16:
1　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是将活神供应给寻求祂的人─诗一一九2、88。
1.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to minister the living God to His seekers—Psa. 119:2, 88.
2　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是将神自己作为生命和光，分赐到那些爱神的话之人里面─25、50、107、116、130、154节。
2.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to dispense God Himself as life and light into those who love the word—vv. 25, 50, 107, 116, 130, 154.
3　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是苏醒人的魂，快活人的心─十九7～8。
3.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to restore man's soul and make man's heart joyous—19:7-8.
4　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是带来救恩─一一九41、170。
4.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to bring us salvation—119:41, 170.
5　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是使我们坚立（28），安慰我们（76），并滋养我们（103）。─引用经文
5.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to strengthen (v. 28), comfort (v. 76), and nourish us (v. 103).
6　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是扶持我们，使我们得救，并使我们有盼望─116～117、49节。
6.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to uphold us, keep us safe, and cause us to hope—vv. 116-117, 49.
7　神活的话，基督的话，使我们享受神作我们的业分─57节。
7.　God's living word, the word of Christ, causes us to enjoy God as our portion—v. 57.
8　神活的话，基督的话，使我们享受神的面（58），以及祂脸上的光照（135）。─引用经文
8.　God's living word, the word of Christ, causes us to enjoy God's countenance (v. 58) and the shining of His face (v. 135).
9　神活的话，基督的话，使我们享受神作我们的藏身之处和盾牌（114），也享受神的帮助和善待（175、65）。─引用经文
9.　God's living word, the word of Christ, causes us to enjoy God as our hiding place and shield (v. 114) and also enjoy God's help and well-dealing (vv. 175, 65).
10　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是使我们有智慧并且通达─98～99节。
10.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to make us wise and give us under-standing—vv. 98-99.
11　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是赐给我们正确的明辨和知识─66节。
11.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to give us proper discernment and knowledge—v. 66.
12　神活的话，基督的话，其功用是保守我们不犯罪，不走一切的邪路─11、101节。
12.　God's living word, the word of Christ, functions to keep us from sinning and from every evil way—vv. 11, 101.
13　神活的话，基督的话，保守我们不绊跌（165），使我们的脚步稳当，并使我们胜过罪孽─133节。
13.　God's living word, the word of Christ, keeps us from stumbling (v. 165), establishes our footsteps, and causes us to overcome iniquity (v. 133).
14　神活的话，基督的话，纯净我们并将我们美化为祂的新妇─十二6，一一九140，弗五26～27，赛六十7下，21，诗二七4。
14.　God's living word, the word of Christ, purifies us and beautifies us to be His bride— 12:6; 119:140; Eph. 5:26-27; Isa. 60:7b, 21; Psa. 27:4.
四　神的话在我们的经历中对我们是不是光，乃在于我们来到神话语前的态度和光景─约五39～40：
D.　Whether or not God's word is a light to us in our experience depends on our attitude and condition in coming to the Word—John 5:39-40:
1　我们需要谦卑自己，不信靠自己，只仰望主的怜悯─赛五七15，六六2。
1.　We need to humble ourselves, having no confidence in ourselves but looking to the Lord for mercy—Isa. 57:15; 66:2.
2　我们全人的各部分应当敞开，接受主的光照─箴二十27。
2.　All the chambers of our inner being should be open to receive the Lord's shining— Prov. 20:27.
五　我们不该制造光，乃该倚靠主光照我们─赛五十10～11。
E.　We should not manufacture light; instead, we should rely on the Lord to enlighten us— Isa. 50:10-11.
叁　“你们要坚定持续的祷告”─西四2～4：
III.　"Persevere in prayer"—Col. 4:2-4:
一　我们若照着主在路加十一章一至十三节的教导祷告，结果我们就会把自己祷告到神里面：─引用经文
A.　If we pray according to the Lord's instructions in Luke 11:1-13, the result will be that we pray ourselves into God:
1　在我们的经历中，我们常受打岔离开神；我们没有住在神里面─我们没有停留在神里面；这就是为什么我们需要把自己祷告到神里面。
1.　Often in our experience we are distracted from God; we do not stay in God—we do not remain in Him; this is why we need to pray ourselves into God.
2　因为我们很容易受打岔离开神，所以我们应当每天早晨花时间与祂同在，把自己祷告到祂里面─诗五3，赛五十4。
2.　Because we are easily distracted from God, we should spend time every morning with Him, praying ourselves into Him—Psa. 5:3; Isa. 50:4.
3　我们祷告的方式若打岔我们，使我们离开主，没有把我们带到主里面，我们祷告的方式就当改变，好把自己祷告到祂里面。
3.　If our way of praying distracts us from the Lord and does not bring us into Him, we should change our way of praying so that we pray ourselves into Him.
4　当我们把自己祷告到神里面，我们就领受祂的丰富（由饼、鱼和鸡蛋所代表）到我们里面，作我们的供应─路十一5～13。
4.　When we pray ourselves into God, we receive His riches (represented by the loaves, the fish, and the egg) into our being for our supply—Luke 11:5-13.
5　饼代表地上的丰富；鱼代表海里的丰富；鸡蛋代表空中与地上之物的丰富；圣灵是这些丰富的总和。
5.　Loaves represent the riches of the land; fish, the riches of the sea; and eggs, the riches of something both in the air and on the earth; the Holy Spirit is the totality of these riches.
6　当我们把自己祷告到神里面，而停留在神里面，我们就接受圣灵作我们生命的供应（由饼、鱼和鸡蛋所表征），使我们能喂养自己，也能喂养一切受我们照顾的人─太二四45～46，约壹五16上，林后三6，徒六4。
6.　When we have prayed ourselves into God to remain in Him, we receive the Holy Spirit as our life supply (signified by the loaves, the fish, and the egg) so that we can feed ourselves and all those under our care—Matt. 24:45-46; 1 John 5:16a; 2 Cor. 3:6; Acts 6:4.
7　我们需要有充分的时间祷告，以确定并有效能的方式私下、隐密的接触主─路十一13，太十四22～23，六6。
7.　We need to allow adequate time for prayer, contacting Him privately and secretly in a definite and prevailing way—Luke 11:13; Matt. 14:22-23; 6:6.
二　祷告的意思是说，我们看见自己一无所是，一无所能；这含示祷告是真正的否认己─可八34，九29，西四2，加二20，腓三3，四6～7、11～13。
B.　To pray means that we realize that we are nothing and that we can do nothing; this implies that prayer is the real denial of the self—Mark 8:34; 9:29; Col. 4:2; Gal. 2:20; Phil. 3:3; 4:6-7, 11-13.
三　祷告实际上就是宣告：“不再是我，乃是基督；”我们的祷告见证我们没有靠自己的努力，去应付任何处境─加二20，罗十12～13。
C.　To pray is actually to declare, "No longer I, but Christ"; our prayer testifies that we do not exercise our self-effort to deal with any situation—Gal. 2:20; Rom. 10:12-13.
四　即使在最小的事上，我们都需要求问主；这样作，就是坚定持续的祷告，并因此而活基督─诗二七4，参书九14，腓四7～8。
D.　Even in the smallest details we need to inquire of the Lord; to do this is to persevere in prayer and thereby to live Christ—Psa. 27:4; cf. Josh. 9:14; Phil. 4:7-8.
五　我们需要划出定时祷告的时间；我们的态度应当把祷告当作我们最重要的事，不让任何的事情打岔─但六10，徒十二5、12。
E.　We need to set aside definite times for prayer; our attitude should be that prayer is our most important business and that nothing should be allowed to interfere with it—Dan. 6:10; Acts 12:5, 12.
六　我们要神垂听我们的祷告，就必须向着圣地、圣城、和圣殿所表征之神的权益祷告─王上八48：
F.　In order for God to listen to our prayers, we need to pray toward God's interests, signified by the Holy Land, the holy city, and the holy temple—1 Kings 8:48:
1　圣地，预表基督是神分给信徒的分（西一12，二6～7，申八7）；圣城，表征在基督里神的国（诗四八1～2）；圣殿，表征神在地上的家，召会（弗二21，提前三15）。─引用经文
1.　The Holy Land typifies Christ as the portion allotted by God to the believers (Col. 1:12; 2:6-7; Deut. 8:7); the holy city signifies the kingdom of God in Christ (Psa. 48:1-2); and the holy temple signifies God's house, the church, on the earth (Eph. 2:21; 1 Tim. 3:15).
2　在被掳到巴比伦期间，但以理把窗户开向耶路撒冷，一日三次祷告；这指明当我们向神的祷告是向着神永远经纶里的目标，就是基督、神的国、与神的家时，神必垂听我们的祷告─但六10。
2.　During the Babylonian captivity Daniel prayed three times a day by opening his windows toward Jerusalem; this indicates that God will listen to our prayer when our prayer to God is toward Christ, the kingdom of God, and the house of God as the goal in God's eternal economy—Dan. 6:10.
3　这意思是说，不论我们为谁祷告，我们的祷告都该对准神的权益，就是对准基督与召会─神在地上的权益，以完成神的经纶。
3.　This means that no matter for whom we are praying, our prayers should be aimed at the interests of God, that is, at Christ and the church as God's interests on earth, for the fulfilling of God's economy.
肆　我们借着坚定持续的祷告而受基督的平安管治，并被基督的话内住，祂就以祂自己浸润我们，并顶替我们，直到我们一切天然的区别都被消除，我们就在实际里成为新人─西三15～17，四2～3，三10～11。
IV.　As we are ruled by the peace of Christ and inhabited by the word of Christ through persevering in prayer, He permeates and replaces us with Himself until all our natural distinctions have been eliminated and we become the new man in reality— Col. 3:15-17; 4:2-3; 3:10-11.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第十五篇　十字架上的争战，以及基督是我们的生命
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：西二15，三4，加二20
壹　在十字架上有争战，如歌罗西二章十五节所启示的：“既将执政的和掌权的脱下，神就把他们公然示众，仗着十字架在凯旋中向他们夸胜”：
一　这节描绘在基督钉十字架的时候所进行的争战：
1　基督在钉十字架的时候，作工要完成救赎；父神也在作工，要审判罪。
2　在那同时，执政的和掌权的也忙着企图阻挠神与基督的工作。
3　歌罗西二章十五节说到夸胜，含示争战；这指明争战在激烈进行着。
4　基督在十字架的工作里，使执政的和掌权的被神脱下，神且把他们公然示众，仗着十字架在凯旋中向他们夸胜。
5　这就是说，祂公开的羞辱了他们；人无法看见这看不见的景象，但所有的天使，无论是好的或坏的，都看见这事。
6　“脱下”意思是撒但什么都抓不牢，保不住。
7　基督对付了撒但邪恶的权势；“祂…为要借着死，废除那掌死权的，就是魔鬼”─来二14下。
8　祂进入死与死战，胜了死权，于是得胜大功告成。
9　这是何等大的一件事！
二　歌罗西二章十五节里的“神”指十二节里的神：─引用经文
1　基督在十字架上时，神涂抹了律法的规条。
2　被用以暴露我们的罪的律法，已经被钉在十字架上了。
3　在基督钉十字架的时候，在神与执政的和掌权的─作撒但属下，为他作工的邪恶天使─之间，有一场看不见的属灵冲突。
4　神赢得了胜利！
5　在主钉十字架时，十字架是宇宙的中心：
ａ　神在那里审判罪和一切消极的事物，并将律法钉在十字架上。
ｂ　祂这样作的时候，执政的和掌权的聚集在神与基督周围。
ｃ　神与基督都在作工：
㈠　基督的工作是被钉十字架。
㈡　神的工作是将执政的和掌权的脱下、脱去。
ｄ　聚集在神与基督周围的执政的和掌权的也在作工，要阻挠神与基督的工作。
ｅ　他们若不是靠得那么近，神怎能脱下他们？
ｆ　歌罗西二章十五节里“将执政的和掌权的脱下”这话指明，他们靠得很近，就像我们的外衣与我们的身体那样近。─引用经文
三　既然律法与邪恶的天使已被摆在一边，神就有清楚的立场和平安的环境，点活祂所拣选的人，就是祂的信徒：
1　祂有合式的气氛完成愉快的工作，就是将自己分赐到祂在已过的永远所拣选的人里面。
2　三一神既将执政的和掌权的脱下，就作为赐生命的灵，借着将祂自己分赐到我们里面，赐生命给我们。
贰　基督是我们的生命─三4，加二20：
一　神的生命就是基督的生命，基督的生命又成了我们的生命─西三4，约五26：
1　基督是我们的生命，意思就是说，祂对我们是主观到了极点的─一4，十四6上，十10下，林前十五45下，罗八10、6、11。
2　不可能把一个人和他的生命分开，因为人的生命就是人自己；因此，说基督是我们的生命，意思就是说，基督成了我们，我们与祂同有一个生命和生活─约十四6上，腓一21上。
3　基督是信徒的生命有三种特点：
ａ　这生命是钉十字架的生命─加二20。
ｂ　这生命是复活的生命─约十一25。
ｃ　这生命是藏在神里面的生命─西三3，太六1～6、16～18。
二　在加拉太二章二十节，我们看见神新约经纶中最基本的真理：─引用经文
1　按照神的经纶，我们不该再活着；反之，基督应当在我们里面活着。
2　在神的经纶里，神的心意是要把经过过程的三一神，作到我们全人里面，使我们成为新人，就是新“我”。
3　我们重生的人，有旧“我”和新“我”；旧“我”已经了结了，但新“我”是活着的：
ａ　已经了结的“我”，是没有神性的“我”。
ｂ　仍然活着的“我”，是加进了神的“我”。
ｃ　旧“我”没有神的成分在其中，新“我”却得着了神圣的生命。
ｄ　旧“我”因着神加到里面作生命，就成了新“我”。
ｅ　新“我”就是旧“我”复活加上神，所产生的“我”。
4　我们与基督并没有两个生命；反之，我们同有一个生命，同过一个生活：
ａ　我们凭祂活着，祂也活在我们里面─约六57。
ｂ　如果我们不活，祂就不活；如果祂不活，我们也不能活。
5　“我”，天然的人，倾向守律法以得完全（腓三6），但神要我们活基督，使神借着基督能从我们得着彰显；因此，神的经纶乃是，“我”在基督的死里被钉死，基督在祂的复活里活在我们里面。─引用经文
6　守律法，是在我们的生活中高举律法在一切之上；活基督，是在我们的生活中使基督作中心和一切。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
THE CRUCIAL POINTS OF THE TRUTH IN PAUL'S EPISTLES— PHILIPPIANS AND COLOSSIANS
Message Fifteen
Warfare at the Cross and Christ Being Our Life
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: Col. 2:15; 3:4; Gal. 2:20
I.　There was warfare at the cross as revealed in Colossians 2:15: "Stripping off the rulers and the authorities, He [God] made a display of them openly, triumphing over them in it [the cross]":
A.　This verse portrays the warfare that took place at the time of Christ's crucifixion:
1.　In His crucifixion Christ was working to accomplish redemption, and God the Father was also working to judge sin.
2.　At the same time the rulers and authorities were busy in the attempt to frustrate the work of God and Christ.
3.　The reference to triumph in Colossians 2:15 implies fighting; it indicates that a war was raging.
4.　In His work on the cross, Christ caused the rulers and authorities to be stripped off, to be made a display of openly, and to be triumphed over in the cross by God.
5.　This means that He shamed them openly; man could not see this invisible scene, but all the angels, both good and bad, saw it.
6.　The words stripping off mean that Satan could not lay hold of anything or keep anything.
7.　Christ dealt with Satan's evil power, "that through death He might destroy him who has the might of death, that is, the devil"—Heb. 2:14c.
8.　He went into death, fought with death, overcame the power of death, and then emerged victorious over everything.
9.　What a great matter this is!
B.　The pronoun He in Colossians 2:15 refers to God in verse 12:
1.　When Christ was on the cross, God wiped out the ordinances of the law.
2.　The law that was used to expose our sinfulness has been nailed to the cross.
3.　During the time of Christ's crucifixion, there was an invisible spiritual conflict between God and the rulers and authorities—evil angels that are subordinates of Satan working for him.
4.　God won the victory!
5.　At the time of Christ's crucifixion, the cross was the center of the universe:
a.　God was judging sin and all negative things and nailing the law to the cross.
b.　As He was doing this, the rulers and authorities gathered around God and Christ.
c.　Both God and Christ were working:
(1)　Christ's work was His crucifixion.
(2)　God's work was to strip off, put off, the rulers and authorities.
d.　The rulers and authorities who were swarming around God and Christ were also working to interfere.
e.　If they had not pressed in closely, how could God have stripped them off?
f.　The words stripping off the rulers and the authorities in Colossians 2:15 indicate that they were very close, as close as our garments are to our body.
C.　Now that the law and the evil angels have been set aside, God has a clear ground and a peaceful environment to enliven His chosen ones, His believers:
1.　He has a proper atmosphere to carry out the pleasant task of dispensing Himself into the ones He chose in eternity past.
2.　As the life-giving Spirit, the Triune God, having stripped off the rulers and authorities, is giving life to us by dispensing Himself into our being.
II.　Christ is our life—3:4; Gal. 2:20:
A.　The life of God is the life of Christ, and the life of Christ has become our life—Col. 3:4; John 5:26:
1.　For Christ to be our life means that He is subjective to us to the uttermost—1:4; 14:6a; 10:10b; 1 Cor. 15:45b; Rom. 8:10, 6, 11.
2.　It is impossible to separate a person from the life of that person, for a person's life is the person himself; thus, to say that Christ is our life means that Christ has become us and that we have one life and one living with Him—John 14:6a; Phil. 1:21a.
3.　With Christ as the believers' life there are three characteristics:
a.　This life is a crucified life—Gal. 2:20.
b.　This life is a resurrected life—John 11:25.
c.　This life is a life hidden in God—Col. 3:3; Matt. 6:1-6, 16-18.
B.　In Galatians 2:20 we see the most basic truth of God's New Testament economy:
1.　According to God's economy, we should no longer live; rather, Christ should live in us.
2.　In His economy God's intention is for the processed Triune God to be wrought into our being to make us a new person, a new "I."
3.　As regenerated people, we have both an old "I" and a new "I"; the old "I" has been terminated, but the new "I" lives:
a.　The "I" who has been terminated is the "I" who was without divinity.
b.　The "I" who still lives is the "I" into which God has been added.
c.　The old "I" had nothing of God in it, whereas the new "I" has received the divine life.
d.　The old "I" has become the new "I" because God as life has been added to it.
e.　The new "I" is the "I" who came into being when the old "I" was resurrected and God was added to it.
4.　We and Christ do not have two lives; rather, we have one life and one living:
a.　We live by Him, and He lives in us—John 6:57.
b.　If we do not live, He does not live, and if He does not live, we cannot live.
5.　"I," the natural person, is inclined to keep the law that it might be perfect (Phil. 3:6), but God wants us to live Christ so that God may be expressed in us through Him; hence, God's economy is that "I" be crucified in Christ's death and that Christ live in us in His resurrection.
6.　To keep the law is to exalt it above all things in our life; to live Christ is to make Him the center and everything in our life.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十五篇　十字架上的争战，以及基督是我们的生命
Warfare at the Cross and Christ Being Our Life
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：西二15，三4，加二20
壹　在十字架上有争战，如歌罗西二章十五节所启示的：“既将执政的和掌权的脱下，神就把他们公然示众，仗着十字架在凯旋中向他们夸胜”：
I.　There was warfare at the cross as revealed in Colossians 2:15: "Stripping off the rulers and the authorities, He [God] made a display of them openly, triumphing over them in it [the cross]":
一　这节描绘在基督钉十字架的时候所进行的争战：
A.　This verse portrays the warfare that took place at the time of Christ's crucifixion:
1　基督在钉十字架的时候，作工要完成救赎；父神也在作工，要审判罪。
1.　In His crucifixion Christ was working to accomplish redemption, and God the Father was also working to judge sin.
2　在那同时，执政的和掌权的也忙着企图阻挠神与基督的工作。
2.　At the same time the rulers and authorities were busy in the attempt to frustrate the work of God and Christ.
3　歌罗西二章十五节说到夸胜，含示争战；这指明争战在激烈进行着。
3.　The reference to triumph in Colossians 2:15 implies fighting; it indicates that a war was raging.
4　基督在十字架的工作里，使执政的和掌权的被神脱下，神且把他们公然示众，仗着十字架在凯旋中向他们夸胜。
4.　In His work on the cross, Christ caused the rulers and authorities to be stripped off, to be made a display of openly, and to be triumphed over in the cross by God.
5　这就是说，祂公开的羞辱了他们；人无法看见这看不见的景象，但所有的天使，无论是好的或坏的，都看见这事。
5.　This means that He shamed them openly; man could not see this invisible scene, but all the angels, both good and bad, saw it.
6　“脱下”意思是撒但什么都抓不牢，保不住。
6.　The words stripping off mean that Satan could not lay hold of anything or keep anything.
7　基督对付了撒但邪恶的权势；“祂…为要借着死，废除那掌死权的，就是魔鬼”─来二14下。
7.　Christ dealt with Satan's evil power, "that through death He might destroy him who has the might of death, that is, the devil"—Heb. 2:14c.
8　祂进入死与死战，胜了死权，于是得胜大功告成。
8.　He went into death, fought with death, overcame the power of death, and then emerged victorious over everything.
9　这是何等大的一件事！
9.　What a great matter this is!
二　歌罗西二章十五节里的“神”指十二节里的神：─引用经文
B.　The pronoun He in Colossians 2:15 refers to God in verse 12:
1　基督在十字架上时，神涂抹了律法的规条。
1.　When Christ was on the cross, God wiped out the ordinances of the law.
2　被用以暴露我们的罪的律法，已经被钉在十字架上了。
2.　The law that was used to expose our sinfulness has been nailed to the cross.
3　在基督钉十字架的时候，在神与执政的和掌权的─作撒但属下，为他作工的邪恶天使─之间，有一场看不见的属灵冲突。
3.　During the time of Christ's crucifixion, there was an invisible spiritual conflict between God and the rulers and authorities—evil angels that are subordinates of Satan working for him.
4　神赢得了胜利！
4.　God won the victory!
5　在主钉十字架时，十字架是宇宙的中心：
5.　At the time of Christ's crucifixion, the cross was the center of the universe:
ａ　神在那里审判罪和一切消极的事物，并将律法钉在十字架上。
a.　God was judging sin and all negative things and nailing the law to the cross.
ｂ　祂这样作的时候，执政的和掌权的聚集在神与基督周围。
b.　As He was doing this, the rulers and authorities gathered around God and Christ.
ｃ　神与基督都在作工：
c.　Both God and Christ were working:
㈠　基督的工作是被钉十字架。
(1)　Christ's work was His crucifixion.
㈡　神的工作是将执政的和掌权的脱下、脱去。
(2)　God's work was to strip off, put off, the rulers and authorities.
ｄ　聚集在神与基督周围的执政的和掌权的也在作工，要阻挠神与基督的工作。
d.　The rulers and authorities who were swarming around God and Christ were also working to interfere.
ｅ　他们若不是靠得那么近，神怎能脱下他们？
e.　If they had not pressed in closely, how could God have stripped them off?
ｆ　歌罗西二章十五节里“将执政的和掌权的脱下”这话指明，他们靠得很近，就像我们的外衣与我们的身体那样近。─引用经文
f.　The words stripping off the rulers and the authorities in Colossians 2:15 indicate that they were very close, as close as our garments are to our body.
三　既然律法与邪恶的天使已被摆在一边，神就有清楚的立场和平安的环境，点活祂所拣选的人，就是祂的信徒：
C.　Now that the law and the evil angels have been set aside, God has a clear ground and a peaceful environment to enliven His chosen ones, His believers:
1　祂有合式的气氛完成愉快的工作，就是将自己分赐到祂在已过的永远所拣选的人里面。
1.　He has a proper atmosphere to carry out the pleasant task of dispensing Himself into the ones He chose in eternity past.
2　三一神既将执政的和掌权的脱下，就作为赐生命的灵，借着将祂自己分赐到我们里面，赐生命给我们。
2.　As the life-giving Spirit, the Triune God, having stripped off the rulers and authorities, is giving life to us by dispensing Himself into our being.
贰　基督是我们的生命─三4，加二20：
II.　Christ is our life—3:4; Gal. 2:20:
一　神的生命就是基督的生命，基督的生命又成了我们的生命─西三4，约五26：
A.　The life of God is the life of Christ, and the life of Christ has become our life—Col. 3:4; John 5:26:
1　基督是我们的生命，意思就是说，祂对我们是主观到了极点的─一4，十四6上，十10下，林前十五45下，罗八10、6、11。
1.　For Christ to be our life means that He is subjective to us to the uttermost—1:4; 14:6a; 10:10b; 1 Cor. 15:45b; Rom. 8:10, 6, 11.
2　不可能把一个人和他的生命分开，因为人的生命就是人自己；因此，说基督是我们的生命，意思就是说，基督成了我们，我们与祂同有一个生命和生活─约十四6上，腓一21上。
2.　It is impossible to separate a person from the life of that person, for a person's life is the person himself; thus, to say that Christ is our life means that Christ has become us and that we have one life and one living with Him—John 14:6a; Phil. 1:21a.
3　基督是信徒的生命有三种特点：
3.　With Christ as the believers' life there are three characteristics:
ａ　这生命是钉十字架的生命─加二20。
a.　This life is a crucified life—Gal. 2:20.
ｂ　这生命是复活的生命─约十一25。
b.　This life is a resurrected life—John 11:25.
ｃ　这生命是藏在神里面的生命─西三3，太六1～6、16～18。
c.　This life is a life hidden in God—Col. 3:3; Matt. 6:1-6, 16-18.
二　在加拉太二章二十节，我们看见神新约经纶中最基本的真理：─引用经文
B.　In Galatians 2:20 we see the most basic truth of God's New Testament economy:
1　按照神的经纶，我们不该再活着；反之，基督应当在我们里面活着。
1.　According to God's economy, we should no longer live; rather, Christ should live in us.
2　在神的经纶里，神的心意是要把经过过程的三一神，作到我们全人里面，使我们成为新人，就是新“我”。
2.　In His economy God's intention is for the processed Triune God to be wrought into our being to make us a new person, a new "I."
3　我们重生的人，有旧“我”和新“我”；旧“我”已经了结了，但新“我”是活着的：
3.　As regenerated people, we have both an old "I" and a new "I"; the old "I" has been terminated, but the new "I" lives:
ａ　已经了结的“我”，是没有神性的“我”。
a.　The "I" who has been terminated is the "I" who was without divinity.
ｂ　仍然活着的“我”，是加进了神的“我”。
b.　The "I" who still lives is the "I" into which God has been added.
ｃ　旧“我”没有神的成分在其中，新“我”却得着了神圣的生命。
c.　The old "I" had nothing of God in it, whereas the new "I" has received the divine life.
ｄ　旧“我”因着神加到里面作生命，就成了新“我”。
d.　The old "I" has become the new "I" because God as life has been added to it.
ｅ　新“我”就是旧“我”复活加上神，所产生的“我”。
e.　The new "I" is the "I" who came into being when the old "I" was resurrected and God was added to it.
4　我们与基督并没有两个生命；反之，我们同有一个生命，同过一个生活：
4.　We and Christ do not have two lives; rather, we have one life and one living:
ａ　我们凭祂活着，祂也活在我们里面─约六57。
a.　We live by Him, and He lives in us—John 6:57.
ｂ　如果我们不活，祂就不活；如果祂不活，我们也不能活。
b.　If we do not live, He does not live, and if He does not live, we cannot live.
5　“我”，天然的人，倾向守律法以得完全（腓三6），但神要我们活基督，使神借着基督能从我们得着彰显；因此，神的经纶乃是，“我”在基督的死里被钉死，基督在祂的复活里活在我们里面。─引用经文
5.　"I," the natural person, is inclined to keep the law that it might be perfect (Phil. 3:6), but God wants us to live Christ so that God may be expressed in us through Him; hence, God's economy is that "I" be crucified in Christ's death and that Christ live in us in His resurrection.
6　守律法，是在我们的生活中高举律法在一切之上；活基督，是在我们的生活中使基督作中心和一切。
6.　To keep the law is to exalt it above all things in our life; to live Christ is to make Him the center and everything in our life.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第十六篇　在一切事上让基督居首位
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：西一18下，17下，三11下，启二4～5，二二1～2上
壹　神永远的经纶可比作大轮（参结一15）；基督是轮轴（中心，或神的中心），基督也是轮辋（圆周，或神的普及）─“一切在于基督，主是我一切”（见诗歌三九四首，副歌）。─引用经文
贰　神的目标是使祂的儿子“在万有中居首位”；神的计划是集中于基督作中心；“万有…在祂里面得以维系；”并且“基督是一切，又在一切之内”─西一18下，17下，三11下：
一　神的计划是“要将万有，无论是在诸天之上的，或是在地上的，都在基督里归一于一个元首之下”─弗一10：
1　归一于一个元首之下乃是“向着召会”的（22～23），使基督的身体既得着拯救，脱离那由天使和人的背叛所引起，在死亡和黑暗里宇宙性崩溃的乱堆，就得以分享基督这位元首的一切（创一1～2与2所有注）。─引用经文
2　神将万有在基督里归一于一个元首之下的经纶，是借着把作生命元素的三一神丰盈生命的供应，分赐到召会所有的肢体里面，使他们从死境中起来，并联于身体而成就的─约一4，十四6上，十10下，林前十五45下，罗八10、6、11。
二　神在祂的经纶里管理宇宙，包括地上一切的君王与王国，为要成就祂的定旨，就是基督应该在万有中居首位─但四17、26：
1　要基督居首位，神就需要一班蒙拣选的人与祂配搭合作；在诸天掌权之下，万有都互相效力，叫神的选民得益处，以完成神使基督居首位的定旨─罗八28～29。
2　团体的基督─基督同祂得胜的新妇─作为神所凿的石头，来砸碎人类政权的集大成以后，要变成一座大山，充满全地，使全地成为神的国─但二34～35、44～45，启十七14，十九7～8、11、14、19。
3　基督作为石头，乃是神行动的中心；祂作为山，乃是普及；因此，基督是包罗万有者，就是那在万有中充满万有者─弗一23，四10。
叁　基督必须在我们的基督徒生活中得着首位；在凡事上让主并以祂居首位，就是用起初的爱爱主，受祂的爱困迫，在我们的生活中尊祂为一切─启二4～5，西一18下，林后五14～15，可十二30，诗七三25～26，八十17～19：
一　召会荒凉和堕落的内在原因，乃是基督没有被神的子民高举；他们没有在凡事上让祂居首位，居第一位；没有让基督居首位并尊重且高举祂，乃是堕落和作恶的原因─耶二13。
二　诗篇八十篇十七节说，“愿你的手护庇你右边的人，就是你为自己所坚固的人子；”这节启示基督在神的右边，就是在宇宙的最高处；第一位，最高的地位，首位，已经赐给基督─徒二33，五31，腓二9～11。
三　什么时候神的子民高举基督，让祂在他们生活的每一面居首位，就有恢复和复兴─诗八十18～19。
四　在凡事上让主居首位，以起初的爱爱主，乃是在我们所是并所作的一切上让生命的流，就是主耶稣在我们里面的流居首位；如此祂就在我们里面作照耀者、救赎者、掌权者、涌流者与供应者─结四七1，启二二1～2，二一21下：
1　坐宝座的这一位乃是羔羊神，是我们救赎的神，从祂的宝座有生命水的河流出来，同着生命树作我们的供应和满足；三一神─神、羔羊、和那灵─在祂宝座（祂的元首权柄）之下，将祂自己分赐到我们里面─二二1～2，参约四14下。
2　我们需要祷告：“主，在我的生活中设立你的宝座；在我全人的中心设立你的宝座；主，把我的整个人生和我的日常生活带到你的宝座之下；”我们若每早晨向主献上这样的祷告，立刻就感觉到有个满了神丰富的东西，在我们里面涌流。
3　这宝座实际上就是基督自己，并表征行政权柄和国度；基督在祂行政的权柄里，乃是神家中管理一切的宝座─赛二二23，来四16。
五　我们属灵经历中的最高点乃是有清明的天，其上有宝座─结一22、26～28：
1　我们基督徒有那一种的天，乃在于我们的良心；我们的良心是与我们的天相联的─罗九1，林后一12。
2　当我们与主之间并与彼此之间一无间隔的时候，我们的天就明如水晶，我们就不仅有无亏的良心，也有清洁的良心─徒二四16，提前一5、19，三9，提后一3，参太五8，箴二二11，提后二22。
3　宝座是宇宙的中心并主管治的同在；我们灵里的宝座，事实上就是基督自己─赛二二23，来四16，罗五21，启二二1。
4　我们若有清明的天，就有宝座，我们自然而然就在宝座的管治和掌权之下；神在我们里面有宝座，意思就是神在我们里面有地位掌权─参但四17、25～26，五18～31，赛六1～8。
5　在清明的天以上有宝座，乃是让神在我们基督徒生活中有最高、最显著的地位；在我们属灵经历中达到在清明的天以上有宝座这点，意思就是在凡事上完全服从神的权柄和行政。
6　以西结一章二十六节中“宝座的样式”乃是“像蓝宝石的样子”；蓝宝石是蓝色的，而蓝是天的颜色，指明神管治的同在有属天的情形、气氛和光景─出二四10。
7　神所要的乃是借着人彰显祂自己，并借着人来掌权；祂要人彰显祂，并执行祂的权柄；神完全的救恩是要使我们借着洋溢之恩，并洋溢之义的恩赐，在生命里得救，并在生命中作王─创一26，启十一15，三21，二二3～5，罗五17、21。
六　基督不仅必须在我们的生活中，也必须在我们一切的信息中居首位；“我们不是传自己，乃是传基督耶稣为主，也传自己为耶稣的缘故，作你们的奴仆”─林后四5，参来一3，八1，十二2，诗八十1、17～19，一一○1～7：
1　我们作工，该时常把人拖回到中心来，叫他们看见“基督是主”；我们必须把主耶稣摆在宝座上─参歌一1～4，赛六1、3，约十二41。
2　要传扬这样的信息，我们自己必须先被神打破摔碎，让基督在我们身上居首位；我们的信息就是我们这人─林后四10～13，约十二24～26，参路十二49～50。
3　主的“好”，胜过世人一切的赞美；天上的笑脸，胜过地上一切的怒脸；天上的安慰，胜过地上的眼泪─太二五21、23，耶一7～9、18～19，但四26。
七　要在凡事上让基督居首位，我们对主耶稣就必须有情深的爱；如此，我们的舌头就会是快手的笔，照着我们对祂一切所是的经历和享受，迅速写出我们对祂的爱和赞美─诗四五1～2，林后三3、6。
八　无论地上的情形如何，无论列国在作什么，基督都得胜、亨通的坐车前往；从祂升天那日，祂就开始坐车前往；祂要继续坐车前往，直到祂在得胜里回来─诗四五4～5，赛五20，六1，徒五31，启六2，十九11～16。
九　唯独作王的基督同着在王权上作祂帮助的得胜者在地上掌权，才能解决今天世界的问题（赛四二1～4）；基督的名要借着得胜的圣徒，被万代记念；并且基督要借着祂得胜并同作王的圣徒，得着众民的赞美（诗四五16～17，启二26）。─引用经文
十　锡安所预表的得胜者，乃是滩头堡，主要借以回来据有全地─诗四八2，但二34～35。
十一　“众城门哪，你们要抬起头来；永久的门户阿，你们要被举起；荣耀的王将要进来。那荣耀的王是谁呢？就是刚强大能的耶和华，在争战中有大能的耶和华！…那荣耀的王是谁呢？万军之耶和华─祂是荣耀的王！”─诗二四7～10：
1　众城门是列国的城门，门户是百姓的家门；基督是万国所羡慕的（该二7）；一般说来，万国都在期待基督来临，但基督不会照着我们人的观念很快就来（彼后三8～9）；因此，我们需要抬起头来，恒切的等候并期待祂的来临。─引用经文
2　荣耀的王是万军之耶和华，就是终极完成的三一神具体化身在得胜且要来的基督里（路二一27，太二五31）；耶和华就是耶稣，耶稣就是成为肉体、钉十字架、并复活的三一神，祂是刚强争战且得胜的一位（一21，启五5）。─引用经文
3　祂要在复活里同祂的得胜者回来据有全地作祂的国─但二34～35，七13～14，珥三11，启十一15，十九13～14。
十二　基督的宝座是永永远远的，祂国的权杖是正直的权杖；基督是王，祂爱公义，恨恶邪恶，父神用欢乐的油膏祂，胜过膏祂的同伙─诗四五6～7，来一8～9。
肆　宝座上的这位基督，显出来的样子好像红宝石（其红色表征救赎）和碧玉（其深绿色表征丰盛的生命）；因此，当我们服从基督的元首权柄并服在祂的宝座之下，我们就成为祂在法理救赎和生机拯救上一切所是的受益者，使我们在神丰富的生命中，显出与荣耀之神相同的样子─启四3，二一10～11上，罗五10。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
THE CRUCIAL POINTS OF THE TRUTH IN PAUL'S EPISTLES— PHILIPPIANS AND COLOSSIANS
Message Sixteen
Giving Christ the First Place in All Things
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: Col. 1:18b, 17b; 3:11b; Rev. 2:4-5; 22:1-2a
I.　God's eternal economy can be likened to a great wheel (cf. Ezek. 1:15); Christ is the hub (the center, or God's centrality), and Christ is the rim (the circumference, or God's universality)—"Everything is in Christ, / And Christ is everything" (see chorus of Hymns, #513).
II.　God's goal is for His Son to have "the first place in all things"; God's plan is focused on Christ as the center; "all things cohere in Him," and "Christ is all and in all"—Col. 1:18b, 17b; 3:11b:
A.　God's plan is "to head up all things in Christ, the things in the heavens and the things on the earth, in Him"—Eph. 1:10:
1.　This heading up is "to the church" (vv. 22-23) so that the Body of Christ may share in all that is of Christ as the Head, having been rescued from the heap of the universal collapse in death and darkness, which was caused by the rebellion of the angels and the rebellion of man (Gen. 1:1-2 and all footnotes on v. 2).
2.　God's economy to head up all things in Christ is accomplished through the dispensing of the abundant life supply of the Triune God as the life factor into all the members of the church that they may rise up from the death situation and be attached to the Body—John 1:4; 14:6a; 10:10b; 1 Cor. 15:45b; Rom. 8:10, 6, 11.
B.　In His economy God administrates the universe, including all the kings and the kingdoms on the earth, in order to fulfill His purpose, which is that Christ should be preeminent in all things—Dan. 4:17, 26:
1.　For Christ to be preeminent, God needs a chosen people to coordinate and cooperate with Him; under the rule of the heavens, everything is working together for the good of God's elect for the purpose of making Christ preeminent—Rom. 8:28-29.
2.　After coming as the God-cut stone to crush the aggregate of human government, the corporate Christ—Christ with His overcoming bride—will become a great mountain to fill the whole earth, making the whole earth God's kingdom—Dan. 2:34-35, 44-45; Rev. 17:14; 19:7-8, 11, 14, 19.
3.　As the stone, Christ is the centrality of God's move, and as the mountain, He is the universality; hence, He is the all-inclusive One, the One who fills all in all—Eph. 1:23; 4:10.
III.　Christ must have the first place in our Christian life; to give the Lord the first place in all things is to love the Lord with the first love, being constrained by His love to regard and take Him as everything in our life—Rev. 2:4-5; Col. 1:18b; 2 Cor. 5:14-15; Mark 12:30; Psa. 73:25-26; 80:17-19:
A.　The intrinsic reason for the desolation and degradation of the church is that Christ is not exalted by God's people; they do not give Him the preeminence, the first place, in everything; the failure to give Christ the preeminence and to honor and exalt Him is the cause of degradation and evils—Jer. 2:13.
B.　Psalm 80:17 says, "Let Your hand be upon the man of Your right hand, / Upon the son of man whom You have strengthened for Yourself"; this verse reveals that Christ is at the right hand of God, the highest place in the universe; the first place, the highest position, the preeminence, has been given to Christ—Acts 2:33; 5:31; Phil. 2:9-11.
C.　Whenever God's people exalt Christ, giving Him the preeminence in every aspect of their living, there is restoration and revival—Psa. 80:18-19.
D.　To give the Lord the first place in all things, to love the Lord with the first love, is to give the flow of life, the flow of the Lord Jesus within us, the preeminence in all that we are and do; then He is the shining One, the redeeming One, the reigning One, the flowing One, and the supplying One within us—Ezek. 47:1; Rev. 22:1-2; 21:21b:
1.　The One sitting on the throne is the Lamb-God, our redeeming God, from whose throne proceeds the river of water of life with the tree of life for our supply and satisfaction; the Triune God—God, the Lamb, and the Spirit—dispenses Himself into us under His throne, His headship—22:1-2; cf. John 4:14b.
2.　We need to pray, "Lord, set up Your throne in my life; set up Your throne in the center of my being; Lord, bring my whole life with my daily life under Your throne"; if we offer such a prayer to the Lord every morning, we will immediately sense something full of God's riches flowing within us.
3.　The throne is actually Christ Himself and signifies the administrative authority and the kingdom; Christ in His administrative authority is the throne that governs everything within the house of God—Isa. 22:23; Heb. 4:16.
E.　The highest point in our spiritual experience is having a clear sky with the throne above it— Ezek. 1:22, 26-28:
1.　The kind of sky we have as Christians depends on our conscience; our conscience is connected to our sky—Rom. 9:1; 2 Cor. 1:12.
2.　When there is nothing between us and the Lord and nothing between us and one another, our sky will be crystal clear, and we will have not only a good conscience but also a pure conscience—Acts 24:16; 1 Tim. 1:5, 19; 3:9; 2 Tim. 1:3; cf. Matt. 5:8; Prov. 22:11; 2 Tim. 2:22.
3.　The throne is the center of the universe, and it is the Lord's ruling presence; the throne in our spirit is actually Christ Himself—Isa. 22:23; Heb. 4:16; Rom. 5:21; Rev. 22:1.
4.　If we have a clear sky, the throne will be present, and we will spontaneously be under the ruling and reigning of the throne; for God to have the throne in us means that He has the position to reign in us—cf. Dan. 4:17, 25-26; 5:18-31; Isa. 6:1-8.
5.　To have the throne above a clear sky is to allow God to have the highest and most prominent position in our Christian life; in our spiritual experience, to reach the point of having the throne above a clear sky means that in everything we are completely submissive to God's authority and administration.
6.　In Ezekiel 1:26 "the likeness of a throne" is "like the appearance of a sapphire stone"; a sapphire stone is blue in color, which is a heavenly color, indicating the heavenly situation, atmosphere, and condition of God's ruling presence—Exo. 24:10.
7.　God desires to manifest Himself through man and to reign through man; He wants man to express Him and to exercise His authority; God's complete salvation is for us to be saved in life and to reign in life by the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness—Gen. 1:26; Rev. 11:15; 3:21; 22:3-5; Rom. 5:17, 21.
F.　Christ must have the first place not only in our living but also in all our messages; "we do not preach ourselves but Christ Jesus as Lord, and ourselves as your slaves for Jesus' sake"—2 Cor. 4:5; cf. Heb. 1:3; 8:1; 12:2; Psa. 80:1, 17-19; 110:1-7:
1.　In our work we should continually draw people back to the center and let them see that "Christ is Lord"; we must give the Lord Jesus His place on the throne—cf. S. S. 1:1-4; Isa. 6:1, 3; John 12:41.
2.　In order to give such a message, we ourselves must be broken by God and allow Christ to have the first place in us; our message is just our person—2 Cor. 4:10-13; John 12:24-26; cf. Luke 12:49-50.
3.　The Lord's "well done" surpasses all the praises of the world; the smiling face of heaven surpasses all the angry faces of the earth; the comfort of heaven surpasses all the tears of the earth—Matt. 25:21, 23; Jer. 1:7-9, 18-19; Dan. 4:26.
G.　In order to give Christ the first place in all things, we must have an affectionate love for Him; then our tongue will be the pen of a ready writer, ready to write our love for Him and our praise to Him with our experience and enjoyment of Him according to all that He is—Psa. 45:1-2; 2 Cor. 3:3, 6.
H.　Regardless of what the situation is on earth, regardless of what the nations are doing, Christ is riding on triumphantly, prosperously; from the day of His ascension He began to ride on, and He will continue to ride until He comes back in victory—Psa. 45:4-5; Isa. 5:20; 6:1; Acts 5:31; Rev. 6:2; 19:11-16.
I.　Only Christ the King reigning on the earth with the overcomers as His helpers in the kingship can solve the problems of today's world (Isa. 42:1-4); Christ's name will be remembered in all generations through the overcoming saints; He will be praised by the nations through His overcoming and co-reigning saints (Psa. 45:16-17; Rev. 2:26).
J.　The overcomers, who are typified by Zion, are the beachhead through which the Lord will return to possess the whole earth—Psa. 48:2; Dan. 2:34-35.
K.　"Lift up your heads, O gates; / And be lifted up, O long enduring doors; / And the King of glory will come in. / Who is the King of glory? / Jehovah strong and mighty! / Jehovah mighty in battle!… / Who is this King of glory? / Jehovah of hosts— / He is the King of glory!"—Psa. 24:7-10:
1.　The gates are of the cities of the nations, the doors are of the houses of the people, and Christ is the Desire of all the nations (Hag. 2:7); all the nations, in a general way, are expecting Christ to come, but Christ will not come quickly according to our human concept (2 Pet. 3:8-9); thus, we need to lift up our heads and await and expect His coming with long endurance.
2.　The King of glory is Jehovah of hosts (that is, of armies), the consummated Triune God embodied in the victorious and coming Christ (Luke 21:27; Matt. 25:31); Jehovah is Jesus, and Jesus is the incarnated, crucified, and resurrected Triune God, who is strong in fighting and is victorious (1:21; Rev. 5:5).
3.　He is the One who will come back in resurrection with His overcomers to possess the entire earth as His kingdom—Dan. 2:34-35; 7:13-14; Joel 3:11; Rev. 11:15; 19:13-14.
L.　Christ's throne is forever and ever, and the scepter of uprightness is the scepter of His kingdom; as the King, Christ has loved righteousness and hated wickedness, and God the Father has anointed Him with the oil of gladness above His companions—Psa. 45:6-7; Heb. 1:8-9.
IV.　Christ as the One on the throne of God has the appearance of sardius (its red color signifying redemption) and jasper (its dark green color signifying life in its richness); thus, when we submit ourselves to Christ's headship and are under His throne, we are the beneficiaries of all that He is in His judicial redemption and His organic salvation so that we may bear the same appearance as the God of glory in His rich life—Rev. 4:3; 21:10-11a; Rom. 5:10.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十六篇　在一切事上让基督居首位
Giving Christ the First Place in All Things
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：西一18下，17下，三11下，启二4～5，二二1～2上
壹　神永远的经纶可比作大轮（参结一15）；基督是轮轴（中心，或神的中心），基督也是轮辋（圆周，或神的普及）─“一切在于基督，主是我一切”（见诗歌三九四首，副歌）。─引用经文
I.　God's eternal economy can be likened to a great wheel (cf. Ezek. 1:15); Christ is the hub (the center, or God's centrality), and Christ is the rim (the circumference, or God's universality)—"Everything is in Christ, / And Christ is everything" (see chorus of Hymns, #513).
贰　神的目标是使祂的儿子“在万有中居首位”；神的计划是集中于基督作中心；“万有…在祂里面得以维系；”并且“基督是一切，又在一切之内”─西一18下，17下，三11下：
II.　God's goal is for His Son to have "the first place in all things"; God's plan is focused on Christ as the center; "all things cohere in Him," and "Christ is all and in all"—Col. 1:18b, 17b; 3:11b:
一　神的计划是“要将万有，无论是在诸天之上的，或是在地上的，都在基督里归一于一个元首之下”─弗一10：
A.　God's plan is "to head up all things in Christ, the things in the heavens and the things on the earth, in Him"—Eph. 1:10:
1　归一于一个元首之下乃是“向着召会”的（22～23），使基督的身体既得着拯救，脱离那由天使和人的背叛所引起，在死亡和黑暗里宇宙性崩溃的乱堆，就得以分享基督这位元首的一切（创一1～2与2所有注）。─引用经文
1.　This heading up is "to the church" (vv. 22-23) so that the Body of Christ may share in all that is of Christ as the Head, having been rescued from the heap of the universal collapse in death and darkness, which was caused by the rebellion of the angels and the rebellion of man (Gen. 1:1-2 and all footnotes on v. 2).
2　神将万有在基督里归一于一个元首之下的经纶，是借着把作生命元素的三一神丰盈生命的供应，分赐到召会所有的肢体里面，使他们从死境中起来，并联于身体而成就的─约一4，十四6上，十10下，林前十五45下，罗八10、6、11。
2.　God's economy to head up all things in Christ is accomplished through the dispensing of the abundant life supply of the Triune God as the life factor into all the members of the church that they may rise up from the death situation and be attached to the Body—John 1:4; 14:6a; 10:10b; 1 Cor. 15:45b; Rom. 8:10, 6, 11.
二　神在祂的经纶里管理宇宙，包括地上一切的君王与王国，为要成就祂的定旨，就是基督应该在万有中居首位─但四17、26：
B.　In His economy God administrates the universe, including all the kings and the kingdoms on the earth, in order to fulfill His purpose, which is that Christ should be preeminent in all things—Dan. 4:17, 26:
1　要基督居首位，神就需要一班蒙拣选的人与祂配搭合作；在诸天掌权之下，万有都互相效力，叫神的选民得益处，以完成神使基督居首位的定旨─罗八28～29。
1.　For Christ to be preeminent, God needs a chosen people to coordinate and cooperate with Him; under the rule of the heavens, everything is working together for the good of God's elect for the purpose of making Christ preeminent—Rom. 8:28-29.
2　团体的基督─基督同祂得胜的新妇─作为神所凿的石头，来砸碎人类政权的集大成以后，要变成一座大山，充满全地，使全地成为神的国─但二34～35、44～45，启十七14，十九7～8、11、14、19。
2.　After coming as the God-cut stone to crush the aggregate of human government, the corporate Christ—Christ with His overcoming bride—will become a great mountain to fill the whole earth, making the whole earth God's kingdom—Dan. 2:34-35, 44-45; Rev. 17:14; 19:7-8, 11, 14, 19.
3　基督作为石头，乃是神行动的中心；祂作为山，乃是普及；因此，基督是包罗万有者，就是那在万有中充满万有者─弗一23，四10。
3.　As the stone, Christ is the centrality of God's move, and as the mountain, He is the universality; hence, He is the all-inclusive One, the One who fills all in all—Eph. 1:23; 4:10.
叁　基督必须在我们的基督徒生活中得着首位；在凡事上让主并以祂居首位，就是用起初的爱爱主，受祂的爱困迫，在我们的生活中尊祂为一切─启二4～5，西一18下，林后五14～15，可十二30，诗七三25～26，八十17～19：
III.　Christ must have the first place in our Christian life; to give the Lord the first place in all things is to love the Lord with the first love, being constrained by His love to regard and take Him as everything in our life—Rev. 2:4-5; Col. 1:18b; 2 Cor. 5:14-15; Mark 12:30; Psa. 73:25-26; 80:17-19:
一　召会荒凉和堕落的内在原因，乃是基督没有被神的子民高举；他们没有在凡事上让祂居首位，居第一位；没有让基督居首位并尊重且高举祂，乃是堕落和作恶的原因─耶二13。
A.　The intrinsic reason for the desolation and degradation of the church is that Christ is not exalted by God's people; they do not give Him the preeminence, the first place, in everything; the failure to give Christ the preeminence and to honor and exalt Him is the cause of degradation and evils—Jer. 2:13.
二　诗篇八十篇十七节说，“愿你的手护庇你右边的人，就是你为自己所坚固的人子；”这节启示基督在神的右边，就是在宇宙的最高处；第一位，最高的地位，首位，已经赐给基督─徒二33，五31，腓二9～11。
B.　Psalm 80:17 says, "Let Your hand be upon the man of Your right hand, / Upon the son of man whom You have strengthened for Yourself"; this verse reveals that Christ is at the right hand of God, the highest place in the universe; the first place, the highest position, the preeminence, has been given to Christ—Acts 2:33; 5:31; Phil. 2:9-11.
三　什么时候神的子民高举基督，让祂在他们生活的每一面居首位，就有恢复和复兴─诗八十18～19。
C.　Whenever God's people exalt Christ, giving Him the preeminence in every aspect of their living, there is restoration and revival—Psa. 80:18-19.
四　在凡事上让主居首位，以起初的爱爱主，乃是在我们所是并所作的一切上让生命的流，就是主耶稣在我们里面的流居首位；如此祂就在我们里面作照耀者、救赎者、掌权者、涌流者与供应者─结四七1，启二二1～2，二一21下：
D.　To give the Lord the first place in all things, to love the Lord with the first love, is to give the flow of life, the flow of the Lord Jesus within us, the preeminence in all that we are and do; then He is the shining One, the redeeming One, the reigning One, the flowing One, and the supplying One within us—Ezek. 47:1; Rev. 22:1-2; 21:21b:
1　坐宝座的这一位乃是羔羊神，是我们救赎的神，从祂的宝座有生命水的河流出来，同着生命树作我们的供应和满足；三一神─神、羔羊、和那灵─在祂宝座（祂的元首权柄）之下，将祂自己分赐到我们里面─二二1～2，参约四14下。
1.　The One sitting on the throne is the Lamb-God, our redeeming God, from whose throne proceeds the river of water of life with the tree of life for our supply and satisfaction; the Triune God—God, the Lamb, and the Spirit—dispenses Himself into us under His throne, His headship—22:1-2; cf. John 4:14b.
2　我们需要祷告：“主，在我的生活中设立你的宝座；在我全人的中心设立你的宝座；主，把我的整个人生和我的日常生活带到你的宝座之下；”我们若每早晨向主献上这样的祷告，立刻就感觉到有个满了神丰富的东西，在我们里面涌流。
2.　We need to pray, "Lord, set up Your throne in my life; set up Your throne in the center of my being; Lord, bring my whole life with my daily life under Your throne"; if we offer such a prayer to the Lord every morning, we will immediately sense something full of God's riches flowing within us.
3　这宝座实际上就是基督自己，并表征行政权柄和国度；基督在祂行政的权柄里，乃是神家中管理一切的宝座─赛二二23，来四16。
3.　The throne is actually Christ Himself and signifies the administrative authority and the kingdom; Christ in His administrative authority is the throne that governs everything within the house of God—Isa. 22:23; Heb. 4:16.
五　我们属灵经历中的最高点乃是有清明的天，其上有宝座─结一22、26～28：
E.　The highest point in our spiritual experience is having a clear sky with the throne above it— Ezek. 1:22, 26-28:
1　我们基督徒有那一种的天，乃在于我们的良心；我们的良心是与我们的天相联的─罗九1，林后一12。
1.　The kind of sky we have as Christians depends on our conscience; our conscience is connected to our sky—Rom. 9:1; 2 Cor. 1:12.
2　当我们与主之间并与彼此之间一无间隔的时候，我们的天就明如水晶，我们就不仅有无亏的良心，也有清洁的良心─徒二四16，提前一5、19，三9，提后一3，参太五8，箴二二11，提后二22。
2.　When there is nothing between us and the Lord and nothing between us and one another, our sky will be crystal clear, and we will have not only a good conscience but also a pure conscience—Acts 24:16; 1 Tim. 1:5, 19; 3:9; 2 Tim. 1:3; cf. Matt. 5:8; Prov. 22:11; 2 Tim. 2:22.
3　宝座是宇宙的中心并主管治的同在；我们灵里的宝座，事实上就是基督自己─赛二二23，来四16，罗五21，启二二1。
3.　The throne is the center of the universe, and it is the Lord's ruling presence; the throne in our spirit is actually Christ Himself—Isa. 22:23; Heb. 4:16; Rom. 5:21; Rev. 22:1.
4　我们若有清明的天，就有宝座，我们自然而然就在宝座的管治和掌权之下；神在我们里面有宝座，意思就是神在我们里面有地位掌权─参但四17、25～26，五18～31，赛六1～8。
4.　If we have a clear sky, the throne will be present, and we will spontaneously be under the ruling and reigning of the throne; for God to have the throne in us means that He has the position to reign in us—cf. Dan. 4:17, 25-26; 5:18-31; Isa. 6:1-8.
5　在清明的天以上有宝座，乃是让神在我们基督徒生活中有最高、最显著的地位；在我们属灵经历中达到在清明的天以上有宝座这点，意思就是在凡事上完全服从神的权柄和行政。
5.　To have the throne above a clear sky is to allow God to have the highest and most prominent position in our Christian life; in our spiritual experience, to reach the point of having the throne above a clear sky means that in everything we are completely submissive to God's authority and administration.
6　以西结一章二十六节中“宝座的样式”乃是“像蓝宝石的样子”；蓝宝石是蓝色的，而蓝是天的颜色，指明神管治的同在有属天的情形、气氛和光景─出二四10。
6.　In Ezekiel 1:26 "the likeness of a throne" is "like the appearance of a sapphire stone"; a sapphire stone is blue in color, which is a heavenly color, indicating the heavenly situation, atmosphere, and condition of God's ruling presence—Exo. 24:10.
7　神所要的乃是借着人彰显祂自己，并借着人来掌权；祂要人彰显祂，并执行祂的权柄；神完全的救恩是要使我们借着洋溢之恩，并洋溢之义的恩赐，在生命里得救，并在生命中作王─创一26，启十一15，三21，二二3～5，罗五17、21。
7.　God desires to manifest Himself through man and to reign through man; He wants man to express Him and to exercise His authority; God's complete salvation is for us to be saved in life and to reign in life by the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness—Gen. 1:26; Rev. 11:15; 3:21; 22:3-5; Rom. 5:17, 21.
六　基督不仅必须在我们的生活中，也必须在我们一切的信息中居首位；“我们不是传自己，乃是传基督耶稣为主，也传自己为耶稣的缘故，作你们的奴仆”─林后四5，参来一3，八1，十二2，诗八十1、17～19，一一○1～7：
F.　Christ must have the first place not only in our living but also in all our messages; "we do not preach ourselves but Christ Jesus as Lord, and ourselves as your slaves for Jesus' sake"—2 Cor. 4:5; cf. Heb. 1:3; 8:1; 12:2; Psa. 80:1, 17-19; 110:1-7:
1　我们作工，该时常把人拖回到中心来，叫他们看见“基督是主”；我们必须把主耶稣摆在宝座上─参歌一1～4，赛六1、3，约十二41。
1.　In our work we should continually draw people back to the center and let them see that "Christ is Lord"; we must give the Lord Jesus His place on the throne—cf. S. S. 1:1-4; Isa. 6:1, 3; John 12:41.
2　要传扬这样的信息，我们自己必须先被神打破摔碎，让基督在我们身上居首位；我们的信息就是我们这人─林后四10～13，约十二24～26，参路十二49～50。
2.　In order to give such a message, we ourselves must be broken by God and allow Christ to have the first place in us; our message is just our person—2 Cor. 4:10-13; John 12:24-26; cf. Luke 12:49-50.
3　主的“好”，胜过世人一切的赞美；天上的笑脸，胜过地上一切的怒脸；天上的安慰，胜过地上的眼泪─太二五21、23，耶一7～9、18～19，但四26。
3.　The Lord's "well done" surpasses all the praises of the world; the smiling face of heaven surpasses all the angry faces of the earth; the comfort of heaven surpasses all the tears of the earth—Matt. 25:21, 23; Jer. 1:7-9, 18-19; Dan. 4:26.
七　要在凡事上让基督居首位，我们对主耶稣就必须有情深的爱；如此，我们的舌头就会是快手的笔，照着我们对祂一切所是的经历和享受，迅速写出我们对祂的爱和赞美─诗四五1～2，林后三3、6。
G.　In order to give Christ the first place in all things, we must have an affectionate love for Him; then our tongue will be the pen of a ready writer, ready to write our love for Him and our praise to Him with our experience and enjoyment of Him according to all that He is—Psa. 45:1-2; 2 Cor. 3:3, 6.
八　无论地上的情形如何，无论列国在作什么，基督都得胜、亨通的坐车前往；从祂升天那日，祂就开始坐车前往；祂要继续坐车前往，直到祂在得胜里回来─诗四五4～5，赛五20，六1，徒五31，启六2，十九11～16。
H.　Regardless of what the situation is on earth, regardless of what the nations are doing, Christ is riding on triumphantly, prosperously; from the day of His ascension He began to ride on, and He will continue to ride until He comes back in victory—Psa. 45:4-5; Isa. 5:20; 6:1; Acts 5:31; Rev. 6:2; 19:11-16.
九　唯独作王的基督同着在王权上作祂帮助的得胜者在地上掌权，才能解决今天世界的问题（赛四二1～4）；基督的名要借着得胜的圣徒，被万代记念；并且基督要借着祂得胜并同作王的圣徒，得着众民的赞美（诗四五16～17，启二26）。─引用经文
I.　Only Christ the King reigning on the earth with the overcomers as His helpers in the kingship can solve the problems of today's world (Isa. 42:1-4); Christ's name will be remembered in all generations through the overcoming saints; He will be praised by the nations through His overcoming and co-reigning saints (Psa. 45:16-17; Rev. 2:26).
十　锡安所预表的得胜者，乃是滩头堡，主要借以回来据有全地─诗四八2，但二34～35。
J.　The overcomers, who are typified by Zion, are the beachhead through which the Lord will return to possess the whole earth—Psa. 48:2; Dan. 2:34-35.
十一　“众城门哪，你们要抬起头来；永久的门户阿，你们要被举起；荣耀的王将要进来。那荣耀的王是谁呢？就是刚强大能的耶和华，在争战中有大能的耶和华！…那荣耀的王是谁呢？万军之耶和华─祂是荣耀的王！”─诗二四7～10：
K.　"Lift up your heads, O gates; / And be lifted up, O long enduring doors; / And the King of glory will come in. / Who is the King of glory? / Jehovah strong and mighty! / Jehovah mighty in battle!… / Who is this King of glory? / Jehovah of hosts— / He is the King of glory!"—Psa. 24:7-10:
1　众城门是列国的城门，门户是百姓的家门；基督是万国所羡慕的（该二7）；一般说来，万国都在期待基督来临，但基督不会照着我们人的观念很快就来（彼后三8～9）；因此，我们需要抬起头来，恒切的等候并期待祂的来临。─引用经文
1.　The gates are of the cities of the nations, the doors are of the houses of the people, and Christ is the Desire of all the nations (Hag. 2:7); all the nations, in a general way, are expecting Christ to come, but Christ will not come quickly according to our human concept (2 Pet. 3:8-9); thus, we need to lift up our heads and await and expect His coming with long endurance.
2　荣耀的王是万军之耶和华，就是终极完成的三一神具体化身在得胜且要来的基督里（路二一27，太二五31）；耶和华就是耶稣，耶稣就是成为肉体、钉十字架、并复活的三一神，祂是刚强争战且得胜的一位（一21，启五5）。─引用经文
2.　The King of glory is Jehovah of hosts (that is, of armies), the consummated Triune God embodied in the victorious and coming Christ (Luke 21:27; Matt. 25:31); Jehovah is Jesus, and Jesus is the incarnated, crucified, and resurrected Triune God, who is strong in fighting and is victorious (1:21; Rev. 5:5).
3　祂要在复活里同祂的得胜者回来据有全地作祂的国─但二34～35，七13～14，珥三11，启十一15，十九13～14。
3.　He is the One who will come back in resurrection with His overcomers to possess the entire earth as His kingdom—Dan. 2:34-35; 7:13-14; Joel 3:11; Rev. 11:15; 19:13-14.
十二　基督的宝座是永永远远的，祂国的权杖是正直的权杖；基督是王，祂爱公义，恨恶邪恶，父神用欢乐的油膏祂，胜过膏祂的同伙─诗四五6～7，来一8～9。L.　Christ's throne is forever and ever, and the scepter of uprightness is the scepter of His kingdom; as the King, Christ has loved righteousness and hated wickedness, and God the Father has anointed Him with the oil of gladness above His companions—Psa. 45:6-7; Heb. 1:8-9.>
肆　宝座上的这位基督，显出来的样子好像红宝石（其红色表征救赎）和碧玉（其深绿色表征丰盛的生命）；因此，当我们服从基督的元首权柄并服在祂的宝座之下，我们就成为祂在法理救赎和生机拯救上一切所是的受益者，使我们在神丰富的生命中，显出与荣耀之神相同的样子─启四3，二一10～11上，罗五10。
IV.　Christ as the One on the throne of God has the appearance of sardius (its red color signifying redemption) and jasper (its dark green color signifying life in its richness); thus, when we submit ourselves to Christ's headship and are under His throne, we are the beneficiaries of all that He is in His judicial redemption and His organic salvation so that we may bear the same appearance as the God of glory in His rich life—Rev. 4:3; 21:10-11a; Rom. 5:10.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
标　语（一）
神按着祂的形像，照着祂的样式造人，目的是要人接受祂作生命，并彰显祂的属性；神给人管治权，目的是要征服祂的仇敌，恢复地，并运用祂管理地的权柄。
God's intention in creating man in His image and according to His likeness is that man would receive Him as life and express Him in His attributes, and God's intention in giving man dominion is to subdue His enemy, recover the earth, and exercise His authority over the earth.
生命树作神永远经纶的中心，预表基督这三一神的具体化身，成为三部分人这器皿的生命和生命的供应，使神得着团体的彰显—这是神中心的思想。
The tree of life as the center of God's eternal economy typifies Christ, the embodiment of the Triune God, to be life and the life supply to the tripartite man as a vessel for the corporate expression of God—this is the central thought of God.
当神的子民爱神、花时间在祂的话上与祂交通时，神就将祂的神圣元素注入他们里面，使他们与祂成为一，作祂的配偶，在生命、性情和彰显上，与祂一样。
As God's people love God and spend time to fellowship with Him in His word, God infuses them with His divine element, making them one with Him as His spouse, the same as He is in life, nature, and expression.
女人的后裔乃是单个的基督—祂借着在十字架上的死，伤了蛇—也是团体的基督—就是男孩子，包括基督作头，以及得胜的信徒作身体—要打败神的仇敌，并带进祂的国，使祂永远的定旨得以完成。
The seed of the woman is the individual Christ— the One who bruised the serpent through His death on the cross— and also the corporate Christ—the man-child, including Christ as the Head and the overcoming believers as the Body— who will defeat God's enemy and bring in His kingdom so that His eternal purpose might be accomplished.
标　语（二）
我们需要认识并经历亚伯拉罕的神、以撒的神和雅各的神，而成为神的以色列，就是在三一神里的召会。
We need to know and experience the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob to become the Israel of God, the church in the Triune God.
我们若要照亚伯拉罕信的脚踪而行，就必须是过祭坛和帐棚生活的人，以基督作我们的生命，召会作我们的生活，过得着神传输的生活，把我们的一切奉献给神，并以祂的同在作我们的地图。
If we would walk in the steps of Abraham's faith, we must be those who live the life of the altar and the tent, taking Christ as our life and the church as our living to live a life of being transfused by God, consecrating our all to God, and taking His presence as our road map.
亚伯拉罕的神乃是借着祂的显现，带着呼召，在异象中，在属人的友情里说话的神，向祂在地上亲密的朋友揭示，神按着祂的心愿，渴望祂的朋友成为什么，以及要祂的朋友作什么，以完成神圣三一的永远经纶。
The God of Abraham is the God of speaking in His appearing, with calling, in a vision, and in the human friendship, to unveil to His intimate friend on the earth what He aspired for him to be and what He wanted him to do according to His heart's desire for the accomplishment of the eternal economy for the Divine Trinity.
我们向神献上从祂所接受，并祂所作到我们里面的之后，祂会在复活里将其归还我们，我们也会相信并经历神是复活的神，以完成祂的定旨。
After we offer to God what we have received of Him and what He has wrought into us, He will return it to us in resurrection, and we will believe in and experience God as the God of resurrection for the fulfillment of His purpose.
标　语（三）
雅各的梦乃是神目标的梦，也就是伯特利的梦，神家的梦，这家就是今日的召会，要终极完成于新耶路撒冷，作神和祂所救赎之选民永远的居所。
Jacob's dream was a dream of God's goal, the dream of Bethel, the dream of the house of God, which is the church today and which will consummate in the New Jerusalem as the eternal dwelling place of God and His redeemed elect.
当我们为着神的建造，经历天然生命的破碎，并经过变化时，我们就会有一个重要且根本的转弯，就是从对神个人的经历转到对神团体的经历—经历神作伯特利的神。
After we experience the breaking of our natural life and undergo transformation for God's building, we will make a crucial and radical turn from the individual experience of God to the corporate experience of God—the experience of God as the God of Bethel.
雅各带着祝福说预言论到他的十二个儿子时，他乃是一个神人，就是一个为神所充满、构成、浸透、甚至重组的人；无论他思想什么，都是神的思想；无论他发表什么意见，都是神的意见。
When Jacob prophesied concerning his twelve sons with blessing, he was a God-man, a man filled, constituted, permeated, and even reorganized with God; whatever he thought was God's thought, and whatever opinion he expressed was God's opinion.
神按着祂的形像造人并给人管治权，目的是要人成为神的复制，作祂团体的彰显，并施行神的权柄对付仇敌、恢复地、并带进神的国。
God's intention in creating man in His image and in giving him dominion was that man would become a reproduction of God for His corporate expression and would exercise God's authority to deal with the enemy, recover the earth, and bring in the kingdom.
